Automatically classifies tasks into compliance tiers and enforces appropriate verification.\n\n**Key Benefits**:\n- Single command replaces confusion between `sc:task` and `sc:task-mcp`\n- Automatic tier classification with confidence scoring\n- Appropriate verification for each task type\n- Prevents over-engineering for trivial changes\n- Ensures safety for critical changes\n\n## Triggers\n\nUse `/sc:task` when:\n- Task involves code modifications with downstream impacts\n- Complexity score >0.6 with code modifications\n- Multi-file scope (>2 estimated affected files)\n- Security domain paths detected (auth/, security/, crypto/)\n- Refactoring or system-wide changes requested\n\n**Auto-Suggest Keywords**:\n- High confidence: \"implement feature\", \"refactor system\", \"fix security\", \"add authentication\", \"update database schema\"\n- Moderate confidence: \"add new\", \"create component\", \"update service\", \"modify API\"\n\n## Usage\n\n```bash\n/sc:task [description]                           # Auto-detect all dimensions\n/sc:task [description] --compliance strict       # Force STRICT tier\n/sc:task [description] --compliance light        # Force LIGHT tier\n/sc:task [description] --skip-compliance         # Bypass compliance (escape hatch)\n/sc:task [description] --verify auto             # Auto-select verification\n```\n\n## Behavioral Flow\n\n### 0. Grep/Glob: Find references\n3. find_referencing_symbols: Trace dependencies\n\n**Verification Phase**:\n1. Task (quality-engineer): Spawn verification agent (STRICT only)\n2.    37→            \"tier_sample_counts\": self.tier_sample_counts,\n    38→            \"inconsistencies\": self.inconsistencies,\n    39→        }\n    40→\n    41→\n    42→def stratified_sample(\n    43→    results: list[ClassificationResult],\n    44→    sample_fraction: float = 0.10,\n    45→    seed: int | None = None,\n    46→) -> list[ClassificationResult]:\n    47→    \"\"\"Select a stratified sample of classified files.\n    48→\n    49→    Ensures proportional representation of each tier.\n    50→    Each tier with files gets at least 1 sample.\n    51→\n    52→    Args:\n    53→        results: All classification results.\n    54→        sample_fraction: Fraction to sample (default 10%).\n    55→        seed: Random seed for reproducibility.\n    56→\n    57→    Returns:\n    58→        List of sampled ClassificationResults.\n    59→    \"\"\"\n    60→    if not results:\n    61→        return []\n    62→\n    63→    rng = random.Random(seed)\n    64→\n    65→    by_tier: dict[str, list[ClassificationResult]] = {}\n    66→    for r in results:\n    67→        key = r.tier.value\n    68→        by_tier.setdefault(key, []).append(r)\n    69→\n    70→ 85→\n    86→    return sampled\n    87→\n    88→\n    89→def validate_consistency(\n    90→    results: list[ClassificationResult],\n    91→    classify_fn: Callable[..., ClassificationResult],\n    92→    sample_fraction: float = 0.10,\n    93→    seed: int | None = 42,\n    94→) -> ValidationResult:\n    95→    \"\"\"Run the consistency validation pass.\n    96→\n    97→    Re-classifies a ValidationResult with consistency metrics.\n   107→    \"\"\"\n   108→    sample = stratified_sample(results, sample_fraction, seed)\n   109→\n   110→    consistent = 0\n   111→    inconsistent = 0\n   112→    inconsistencies = []\n   113→    tier_sample_counts: dict[str, int] = {}\n   114→\n   115→    for original in sample:\n   116→        tier_key = original.tier.value\n   117→        tier_sample_counts[tier_key] = tier_sample_counts.get(tier_key, 0) + 1\n   118→\n   119→        # Re-classify with same parameters\n   120→        has_refs = original.action not in (V2Action.DELETE, V2Action.ARCHIVE)\n   121→        re_result = classify_fn(\n   122→            original.file_path,\n   123→            has_references=has_refs,\n   124→        )\n   125→\n   126→        if re_result.tier == original.tier and re_result.action == original.action:\n   127→            consistent += 1\n   128→        else:\n   129→            inconsistent += 1\n   130→            inconsistencies.append({\n   131→                \"file_path\": original.file_path,\n   132→                \"original_tier\": original.tier.value,\n   133→                \"original_action\": original.action.value,\n   134→                \"re_tier\": re_result.tier.value,\n   135→                \"re_action\": re_result.action.value,\n   136→            })\n   137→\n   138→    total = consistent + inconsistent\n   139→    rate = consistent / total if total > 0 else 1.0\n   140→\n   141→    return ValidationResult(\n   142→        total_classified=len(results),\n   143→ keywords.\n\n    Returns a float >= 1.0 (base complexity of 1 + branch count).\n    \"\"\"\n    count = 0\n    for line in content.splitlines():\n        for pat in _BRANCH_PATTERNS:\n            if pat.search(line):\n                count += 1\n                break  # one match per line is enough\n    return 1.0 + count\n\n\ndef _git_file_age(file_path: str, repo_root: str) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Get ISO date of first commit for a file using git log --follow.\n\n    Returns ISO date string or \"unknown\" if git is unavailable.\n    \"\"\"\n    try:\n        result = subprocess.run(\n            [\"git\", \"log\", \"--follow\", \"--diff-filter=A\",\n             \"--format=%aI\", \"--\", file_path],\n            capture_output=True, text=True, cwd=repo_root, timeout=10,\n        )\n pass\n    return \"unknown\"\n\n\ndef _git_file_churn(file_path: str, repo_root: str) -> int:\n    \"\"\"Count total commits touching a file.\n\n    Returns 0 if git is unavailable.\n    \"\"\"\n    try:\n        result = subprocess.run(\n            [\"git\", \"log\", \"--follow\", \"--oneline\", \"--\", file_path],\n            capture_output=True, text=True, cwd=repo_root, timeout=10,\n        )\n        return len(result.stdout.strip().splitlines())\n    except (subprocess.SubprocessError, FileNotFoundError):\n        return 0\n\n\ndef _compute_coupling(\n    file_path: str,\n    all_analyses: dict[str, FileAnalysis],\n) -> float:\n    \"\"\"Compute import in-degree: how many other files import this file.\n\n    Returns ratio: importers / total_files (0.0 to 1.0).\n    \"\"\"\n    total = len(all_analyses)\n    if total <= 1:\n        return 0.0\n\n    # Normalize target for matching\n    base_name = os.path.basename(file_path)\n    stem = os.path.splitext(base_name)[0]\n\n    importers = 0\n    for other_path, analysis in all_analyses.items():\n        if other_path == file_path:\n            continue\n        for imp in analysis.imports:\n            if stem in imp or base_name in imp:\n                importers += 1\n                break\n\n    return round(importers / (total - 1), 4)\n\n\ndef _find_test_coverage(file_path: str, all_files: list[str]) -> float | None:\n    \"\"\"Heuristic test coverage: check if a matching test file exists.\n\n    Returns 1.0 if test file found, 0.0 if no test file found,\n    None for non-source files.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Only compute for source files\n    ext = os.path.splitext(file_path)[1].lower()\n    if ext not in {\".py\", \".js\", \".ts\", \".jsx\", \".tsx\", \".vue\"}:\n        return None\n\n    base = os.path.basename(file_path)\n    stem = os.path.splitext(base)[0]\n\n    # Test file naming conventions\n    test_patterns = [\n        f\"test_{stem}\",\n        f\"{stem}_test\",\n        f\"{stem}.test\",\n        f\"{stem}.spec\",\n    ]\n\n    for other in all_files:\n        other_base = os.path.basename(other).lower()\n \"changelog\", \"contributing\", \"license\", \"index\"):\n            continue\n        if doc_stem not in code_stems:\n            orphaned.append(OrphanedDoc(doc_file=doc_path))\n    return orphaned\n\n\ndef check_style_issues(\n    file_path: str,\n    content: str,\n) -> list[StyleIssue]:\n    \"\"\"Check a doc file for style inconsistencies.\n\n    Checks:\n      1. Heading hierarchy: H1 should appear at most once, levels shouldn't skip.\n      2. Link format: bare URLs without markdown link syntax.\n      3. Code block conventions: unclosed fenced code blocks.\n    \"\"\"\n    issues: list[StyleIssue] = []\n    lines = content.splitlines()\n\n    h1_count = 0\n    last_heading_level = 0\n    in_code_block = False\n    code_block_start = 0\n\n    for i, line in enumerate(lines, start=1):\n        # Track code blocks\n        if line.strip().startswith(\"```\"):\n            if in_code_block:\n                in_code_block = False\n            else:\n                in_code_block = True\n                code_block_start = i\n            continue\n\n        if in_code_block:\n            continue\n\n        # Heading checks\n        hm = _HEADING_PATTERN.match(line)\n        if hm:\n            level = len(hm.group(1))\n            if level == 1:\n                h1_count += 1\n                if h1_count > 1:\n                    issues.append(StyleIssue(\n                        file_path=file_path,\n                        line_number=i,\n                        issue_type=\"heading_hierarchy\",\n                        description=\"Multiple H1 headings\",\n                    ))\n            if last_heading_level > 0 and level > last_heading_level + 1:\n                issues.append(StyleIssue(\n                    file_path=file_path,\n                    line_number=i,\n                    issue_type=\"heading_hierarchy\",\n                    description=f\"Heading level skipped: H{last_heading_level} -> H{level}\",\n                ))\n            last_heading_level = level\n\n        # Bare URL check (URLs not inside markdown link syntax or code)\n        bare_urls = re.findall(r\"(?<!\\()(https?://\\S+)(?!\\))\", line)\n        for url in bare_urls:\n            # Skip if inside a markdown link [text](url)\n            if f\"]({url})\" in line:\n                continue\n            issues.append(StyleIssue(\n                file_path=file_path,\n                line_number=i,\n                issue_type=\"link_format\",\n                description=f\"Bare URL: {url}\",\n            ))\n\n    # Unclosed code block\n    if in_code_block:\n        issues.append(StyleIssue(\n            file_path=file_path,\n            line_number=code_block_start,\n            issue_type=\"code_block_convention\",\n            description=\"Unclosed fenced code block\",\n        ))\n\n    return issues\n\n\ndef full_docs_audit(\n    doc_files: dict[str, str],\n    known_files: set[str],\n    code_files: set[str] | None = None,\n    exported_symbols: dict[str, list[str]] | None = None,\n    last_modified: dict[str, str] | None = None,\n    threshold_days: int = 365,\n    current_date: datetime | None = None,\n) -> FullDocsAuditResult:\n    \"\"\"Run full 5-section docs audit (--pass-docs).\n\n    Args:\n        doc_files: Mapping of doc_file_path -> content.\n        known_files: All known file paths.\n        code_files: Set of code file paths (for orphan detection).\n        exported_symbols: Mapping source_file -> exported symbol names.\n        last_modified: Mapping file_path -> ISO date.\n        threshold_days: Staleness threshold in days.\n        current_date: Current date for staleness check.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Sections 1 & 2: reuse minimal audit\n    minimal = audit_docs(\n        doc_files, known_files, last_modified, threshold_days, current_date,\n    )\n\n    # Section 3: coverage gaps\n    coverage_gaps = detect_coverage_gaps(\n        exported_symbols or {}, doc_files,\n    )\n\n    # Section 4: orphaned docs\n    orphaned = detect_orphaned_docs(doc_files, code_files or set())\n\n    # Section 5: style issues\n    style_issues: list[StyleIssue] = []\n    for file_path, content in doc_files.items():\n        style_issues.extend(check_style_issues(file_path, content))\n\n    return FullDocsAuditResult(\n        broken_links=minimal.broken_links,\n        stale_docs=minimal.stale_docs,\n        coverage_gaps=coverage_gaps,\n        orphaned_docs=orphaned,\n        style_issues=style_issues,\n    )\n","numLines":469,"startLine":1,"totalLines":469}}}
